				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Nun komm, der Heiden Heiland, BWV 62 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1724 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>For the 1st Sunday in Advent,
</p>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<ol><li>Chorale: Nun komm, der Heiden Heiland. "The most splendid movement in the cantata"<sup>1</sup>. A typical Bach chorale setting from this cycle; the chorale melody is sung plain by the sopranos, while the rest of the voices and instruments play in imitation on a related motive. 
</li><li>Aria (Tenor): Bewundert, o Menschen, dies grosse Geheimnis. Another usage of the choral in this movement, a pure expression of joy. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): So geht aus Gottes Herrlichkeit und Thron. Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Aria (Bass): Streite, siege, starker Held! A very sparse texture of continuo with strings at the octave; note that the common time signature contrasts with the bouncy 3/8 of the first aria. In the score, no accompaniment except bc, but accompanied by strings at octave in original parts.
</li><li>Recitativo (Soprano, Alto): Wir ehren diese Herrlichkeit. Recitative with string accompaniment. 
</li><li>Choral: Lob sei Gott, dem Vater, ton. A plain chorale setting. 
</li></ol>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Print_Sources_Consulted">Print Sources Consulted</span></h4>
<ul><li>Dürr, Alfred. <i><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://astore.amazon.com/intemusiscorl-20/detail/0199297762/">The Cantatas of J.S. Bach</a></span></i>. 2 ed. Richard D.P. Jones (Trans). 
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Oxford: Oxford University Press, 2005.
</dd></dl>
